-   [<span data-ttu-id="81e41-107">Transaction jeux cntcnd de documents-CONAPW</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81e41-107">Transaction Sets CNTCND-CONAPW</span></span>](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#cntcnd)

-   [<span data-ttu-id="81e41-110">Transaction jeux cuscar de documents-DEBREC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="81e41-110">Transaction Sets CUSCAR-DEBREC</span></span>](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#cuscar)
